( n56 ) <p> Whereas Newton 's synthetic method sought to capture laws of nature based on a single frame of reference and to apply them in the same manner to all parts of the physical universe , Einstein 's analytical approach sought to describe the theoretical properties of nature invariant to a particular frame of reference. n57 The immediate result of this new trajectory is a radically different perspective on space and time. n58 Pondering the cosmological difficulties of Newton 's work , Einstein remarked on the infinite nature of the universe .

SENTPOS COCA_acad_wlp_2009_03_FILE##4071167 COCA  A    0  325 Although the idea of the Spirit as the symmetry between the Father and the Son , and between Christ and Christians , is preserved , Mhlen framed his Pneumatology no longer in terms of causality but in the context of the divine self-surrender. n164 With this reframing he sought to overcome the limitations of a causal interpretation of existence ( esse extra suam causam ) in order to portray the Spirit as God going beyond himself , the kenosis of God to creation. n165 Lyle Dabney has more recently interpreted the kenosis of the Spirit as the " continuity " between creation and redemption. n166 He criticized Moltmann for his understanding of kenosis that finds in the Spirit merely the object of the act of the Father ( n167 ) --a criticism that also applies to Mhlen 's proposal .
